YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 180-rules system (180 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 180-rules system (180 strict rules).
Removing 180 relatively RFC-match-bounded rules [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, WST 2022].
Remains to prove termination of a 0-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED
